msg:The room is very big, very clean, and the service is also very good. There is free parking, welcome fruit, and a mini bar. Two cups of tea are delivered to the room. A very cute dragon doll is also given for checking in during the Spring Festival. There is a bathtub in the room, and there is a bath set that is charged. It is not expensive, 35 yuan. If you want to take a bath but don't want to spend money, you can bring your own bathtub set. But there are two disadvantages, that is, it is far from the May Day Square, about 5/6 subway stations, but fortunately the hotel is not far from the subway station, about 10 minutes walk, and those who don't want to walk can rent a shared electric donkey, which is super cool. The second disadvantage is that the hot water is not hot enough. Although Changsha was warmer when we went there, we wanted to take a hot bath after a day of shopping. The hot water is not hot enough, which really affects the stay experience. I hope the hotel can improve it. By the way, the hotel is very soundproof, but the bed is a little soft.
